################################################################################
#
# PRAAT COMPLETE CAPABILITY CATALOGUE
# ====================================
# Source: github.com/praat/praat C++ source
#   Command names: praat_addAction/praat_addMenuCommand registration strings
#   Parameters: FORM block parsing, joined to registrations via callback name
# Version: 6.4.62 (March 13, 2026)
# Extraction date: 2026-04-08
#
#   version 3 — 8 April 2026
#
# Command names in §2 are SCRIPTING names — the exact strings that
# Praat's interpreter matches when reading a script. These come from
# the registration layer (praat_addAction calls), NOT from FORM dialog
# titles. FORM dialog titles can differ (e.g., "To Formant (Burg method)"
# in the dialog vs "To Formant (burg)" in scripts).
#
# Parameter defaults are Praat SOURCE CODE defaults — the values Praat
# uses when no argument is supplied. These may differ from clinical
# best-practice values in APPENDIX_D_CLINICAL_DEFAULTS.txt.
#
# To the extent possible under the Praat license, this document is Part of EML
# PraatGen GPL-3.0-or-later — Ian Howell, Embodied Music Lab
#
# CONTENTS:
#   §1  Class hierarchy (object inheritance)
#   §2  All commands with parameters and defaults
#   §3  Formula engine functions (365 entries, categorized)
#
################################################################################


################################################################################
# §1 CLASS HIERARCHY
# Key object types and their inheritance chains.
# Critical insight: Sound IS a Matrix, so Formula: operates on it at C speed.
################################################################################

# Core analysis chain
Sound -> Vector -> Matrix -> SampledXY -> Sampled -> Function -> Daata -> Thing
LongSound -> SampledXY (direct file-backed, not Matrix)
Pitch -> Sampled -> Function
Formant -> Sampled -> Function
Intensity -> Vector -> Matrix
Spectrum -> Matrix
Spectrogram -> Matrix
Harmonicity -> Vector -> Matrix
PointProcess -> Function
TextGrid -> Function
Table -> Daata (NOT Matrix — row/column, not sampled)
TableOfReal -> Daata

# Spectral/cepstral
PowerCepstrogram -> Matrix
PowerCepstrum -> Cepstrum -> Matrix
Ltas -> Vector -> Matrix
Cochleagram -> Matrix

# Tiers (all inherit time-point structure)
PitchTier -> RealTier -> AnyTier -> Function
IntensityTier -> RealTier
DurationTier -> RealTier
AmplitudeTier -> RealTier
FormantGrid -> Function (contains multiple RealTier tracks)

# Synthesis
Manipulation -> Function (contains PitchTier + DurationTier + Sound)
KlattGrid -> Function

# Statistics (David Weenink)
PCA -> Eigen -> Daata
Discriminant -> Daata
Configuration -> TableOfReal
Dissimilarity -> Proximity -> TableOfReal
MixingMatrix -> TableOfReal

# Special
Electroglottogram -> Sound -> Vector -> Matrix
PatternList -> Matrix (neural net input)
ActivationList -> Matrix (neural net output)
DTW -> Matrix


################################################################################
# §2 ALL COMMANDS WITH PARAMETERS AND DEFAULTS
# Command names are SCRIPTING names (from praat_addAction registration).
# These are the exact strings Praat's interpreter matches in scripts.
#
# [alias] = legacy name that still works but is not the current name.
# Defaults are Praat source code defaults, not clinical recommendations.
################################################################################

  LongSound preferences  [alias]
    COMMENT        This setting determines the maximum number of seconds
    COMMENT        for viewing the waveform and playing a sound in the LongSound window.
    COMMENT        The LongSound window can become very slow if you set it too high.

# --- String manipulation (52) ---
  backslashTrigraphsToUnicode$ (string$) – convert e.g. \ct to U+0254
  date# ( ) – current local date and time as a vector
  date$ ( ) – current local date and time

  date_utc$ ( ) – current UTC date and time
  endsWith (string$, part$) – determine whether string$ ends with part$
  endsWith_caseInsensitive (string$, part$) – determine whether string$ ends with part$
  extractLine$ (string$, part$) – everything after the first occurrence of part$
  extractNumber (string$, part$) – the number after the first occurrence of part$
  extractWord$ (string$, part$) – the word after the first occurrence of part$
  fixed$ (number, decimalPlaces) – format a number as a string with a fixed number of decimal places
  hash (string$) – return a numeric hash code for a string
  hex$ (integer) – convert an integer to a hexadecimal string
  hexadecimal$ (integer) – convert an integer to a hexadecimal string (alias for hex$)
  index (string$, part$) – look up a substring, or 0 if not found
  index (strings$#, s$) – look up whether and where s$ first occurs in strings$#
  index_caseInsensitive (string$, part$) – look up a substring, or 0 if not found
  index_caseInsensitive (strings$#, s$) – look up whether and where s$ first occurs in strings$#
  index_regex (string$, regex$) – determine whether and where string$ first matches regex$
  left$ (string$, n) – the n first characters in string$
  length (string$) – number of characters
  lowerCamelCase$ (string$) – convert string to lowerCamelCase
  lowerSnakeCase$ (string$) – convert string to lower_snake_case
  mid$ (string$, from, n) – the n characters in string$, starting at position from
  numberOfColumns – the number of columns in a matrix object or Matrix-like object
  numberOfRows – the number of rows in a matrix object or Matrix-like object
  numbers# (n) – the integers 1 through n (alias for to#)
  percent$ (number, precision) – format a number as a percentage
  replace$ (a$, b$, c$, n) – within a$, replace the first n occurrences of b$ with c$, or all if n = 0
  replace_regex$ (a$, b$, c$, n) – within a$, replace the first n matches of regular expression b$ with the regular expression c$, or all if n = 0
  right$ (string$, n) – the n last characters in string$
  rindex (string$, part$) – look up a substring from the end, or 0 if not found
  rindex (strings$#, s$) – look up whether and where s$ last occurs in strings$#
  rindex_caseInsensitive (string$, part$) – look up a substring from the end, or 0 if not found
  rindex_caseInsensitive (strings$#, s$) – look up whether and where s$ last occurs in strings$#
  rindex_regex (string$, regex$) – determine whether and where string$ last matches regex$
  splitBy$# (string$, separator$) – split a string into a string array by separator
  splitByWhitespace$# (string$) – split a string into inks
  startsWith (string$, part$) – determine whether string$ starts with part$
  startsWith_caseInsensitive (string$, part$) – determine whether string$ starts with part$
  string$ (number) – format a number as a string
  truncateLeft$ (string$, newMaximumWidth [, pad$]) – left truncation of string$
  truncateRight$ (string$, newMaximumWidth [, pad$]) – right truncation of string$
  unhex$ (hexString$) – convert a hexadecimal string back to characters
  unicode (c$) – the Unicode codepoint number that corresponds to character c$
  unicode$ (n) – the character that corresponds to Unicode codepoint n
  unicodeToBackslashTrigraphs$ (string$) – convert e.g. U+0254 to \ct
  upperCamelCase$ (string$) – convert string to UpperCamelCase
  upperCase$ (string$) – turns all lower-case characters into capitals
  upperCaseAppName$ ( ) – the name of the app in upper camel case, e.g. Praat or PraatForHospitals
  upperSnakeCase$ (string$) – convert string to UPPER_SNAKE_CASE
  vertical$ (stringArray$#) – format a string array vertically

  max (a, ...) – maximum
  max (v#) – maximum of elements
  max_e (v#) – maximum element, error if vector is empty
  max_removeUndefined (v#) – maximum element, ignoring undefined values
  mean (v#) – mean of elements
  min (a, ...) – minimum
  min (v#) – minimum of elements
  min_e (v#) – minimum element, error if vector is empty
  min_removeUndefined (v#) – minimum element, ignoring undefined values

  mul_fast## (a##, b##) – fast matrix-matrix multiplication
  mul_metal## (a##, b##) – Metal-accelerated matrix-matrix multiplication (macOS)

  outer## (a#, b#) – outer product of vectors
  peaks## (vector#, includeEdges, interpolation, sortByHeight)
  repeat# (v#, n) – repeat the whole sequence of elements of v# n times
  rowInners# (a##, b##) – row-wise inner products of two matrices
  rowSums# (matrix##)
  shuffle# (vector#) – randomize order
  shuffle$# (stringVector$#) – randomize order

  softmax# (vector#)

  solve# (a##, y#) – find x for which A * x = y
  solve## (a##, y##) – find X for which A * X = Y

  sort# (vector#) – reshuffle in increasing order
  sort$# (stringVector$#) – reshuffle in Unicode-alphabetical order
  sort_numberAware$# (stringVector$#) – reshuffle in Unicode-alphabetical order, with special attention to numbers
  sort_removeUndefined# (v#) – sort in increasing order, removing undefined values
  stdev (v#) – standard deviation of the elements of a vector
  sum (v#) – sum the elements
  sumOver (loopVariable to n, numericExpressionOptionallyUsingLoopVariable) – Sigma
  to# (n) – the integers 1 through n
  transpose## (matrix##) – flip matrix along its diagonal
  zero# (n) – vector with n elements that are all 0
  zero## (nrow, ncol) – matrix with nrow x ncol elements that are all 0

# --- Random number generation (31) ---
  random_initializeSafelyAndUnpredictably ( ) – undoes the effects of the following function
  random_initializeWithSeedUnsafelyButPredictably (seed) – reproducible sequence of random numbers
  randomBernoulli (p) – Bernoulli-distributed random deviate (0 or 1)
  randomBernoulli# (n, p) – n independent Bernoulli-distributed random numbers (0 or 1)
  randomBernoulli# (vector#, p) – duplicate vector#, and replace all elements with independent Bernoulli-distributed random numbers (0 or 1)
  randomBinomial (numberOfTrials, probability) – binomial-distributed random number
  randomGamma (shape, rate) – gamma-distributed random deviate
  randomGamma# (n, shape, rate) – n independent gamma-distributed random numbers
  randomGamma# (vector#, shape, rate) – duplicate vector#, and replace all elements with independent gamma-distributed random numbers
  randomGamma## (matrix##, shape, rate) – duplicate matrix##, and replace all cells with independent gamma-distributed random numbers
  randomGamma## (nrow, ncol, shape, rate) – nrow x ncol independent gamma-distributed random numbers
  randomGauss (mu, sigma) – normally distributed random deviate
  randomGauss# (n, mu, sigma) – n independent normally distributed random numbers
  randomGauss# (vector#, mu, sigma) – duplicate vector#, and replace all elements with independent normally distributed random numbers
  randomGauss## (matrix##, mu, sigma) – duplicate matrix##, and replace all cells with independent normally distributed random numbers
  randomGauss## (nrow, ncol, mu, sigma) – nrow x ncol independent normally distributed random numbers
  randomInteger (min, max) – uniformly distributed random integer
  randomInteger# (n, min, max) – n independent uniformly distributed random integers
  randomInteger# (vector#, min, max) – duplicate vector#, and replace all elements with independent uniformly distributed random integers
  randomInteger## (matrix##, min, max) – duplicate matrix##, and replace all cells with independent uniformly distributed random integers
  randomInteger## (nrow, ncol, min, max) – nrow x ncol independent uniformly distributed random integers
  randomPoisson (mean) – Poisson-distributed random deviate
  randomPoisson# (n, mean) – n independent Poisson-distributed random numbers
  randomPoisson# (vector#, mean) – duplicate vector#, and replace all elements with independent Poisson-distributed random numbers
  randomPoisson## (matrix##, mean) – duplicate matrix##, and replace all cells with independent Poisson-distributed random numbers
  randomPoisson## (nrow, ncol, mean) – nrow x ncol independent Poisson-distributed random numbers
  randomUniform (min, max) – uniformly distributed random deviate
  randomUniform# (n, min, max) – n independent uniformly distributed random numbers
  randomUniform# (vector#, min, max) – duplicate vector#, and replace all elements with independent uniformly distributed random numbers
  randomUniform## (matrix##, min, max) – duplicate matrix##, and replace all cells with independent uniformly distributed random numbers
  randomUniform## (nrow, ncol, min, max) – nrow x ncol independent uniformly distributed random numbers

# --- Selection and object management (19) ---
  minusObject (...) – deselect object(s) in the list
  numberOfSelected ( ) – the number of selected objects
  numberOfSelected (type$) – the number of selected objects of type type$
  objectsAreIdentical (id1, id2) – 1 if the two objects are identical, else 0
  plusObject (...) – select more object(s) in the list
  removeObject (...) – remove objects from the list, by ID and/or name
  selected ( ) – the ID of the topmost selected object
  selected (i) – the ID of the ith selected object (as counted from the top, or from the bottom if negative)
  selected (type$) – the ID of the topmost selected object of type type$
  selected (type$, i) – the ID of the ith selected object of type type$ (as counted from the top, or from the bottom if negative)
  selected# ( ) – the IDs of all selected objects
  selected# (type$) – the IDs of all selected objects of type type$
  selected$ ( ) – the full name (type + given name) of the topmost selected object
  selected$ (i) – the full name (type + given name) of the ith selected object (as counted from the top, or from the bottom if negative)
  selected$ (type$) – the given name of the topmost selected object of type type$
  selected$ (type$, i) – the given name of the ith selected object of type type$ (as counted from the top, or from the bottom if negative)
  selected$# ( ) – the full names of all selected objects
  selected$# (type$) – the given names of all selected objects of type type$
  selectObject (...) – select object(s) in the list by ID and/or full name

# --- File and system (31) ---
  appendFile (filePath$, ...) – write texts, numbers, vectors and so on at the end of an existing file (create such a file if it does not exist yet)
  appendFileLine (filePath$, ...) – write texts, numbers, vectors and so on, followed by a newline, at the end of an existing file (create such a file if it does not exist yet)
  appendInfo (...) – write texts, numbers, vectors and so on, to the Info window
  appendInfoLine (...) – write texts, numbers, vectors and so on, followed by a newline, to the Info window
  createFolder (folderPath$) – create a new folder, or do nothing if it already exists
  defaultDirectory$ – the directory (folder) that Praat will use if you specify no directory
  fileNames$# (path$) – get the names of the files in a directory
  fileReadable (path$) – does a file exist?
  folderNames$# (path$) – get the names of the folders in a directory
  homeDirectory$ – the home directory (folder) of the current user
  preferencesDirectory$ – the Praat preferences directory (folder)
  readFile (filePath$) – read a number from a text file
  readFile# (filePath$) – read a vector from a text file
  readFile## (filePath$) – read a matrix from a text file
  readFile$ (filePath$) – read a whole text file into a string
  readLinesFromFile$# (filePath$) – read all lines from a text file
  runNotebook (filePath$) – run a Praat notebook
  runScript (filePath$, ...) – run a script with the given arguments
  runScriptWithForm (filePath$, ...) – run a script, showing its form dialog
  runSubprocess (executableFilePath$, ...) – run an external program with the given arguments
  runSubprocess$ (executableFilePath$, ...) – run an external program with the given arguments, and return its output
  runSystem (...) – run a system command line with the given arguments concatenated
  runSystem$ (...) – run a system command line with the given arguments concatenated, and return its output
  runSystem_nocheck (...) – run a system command; suppress errors
  setWorkingDirectory (folderPath$) – set the working directory for subsequent file operations
  tryToAppendFile (filePath$) – check whether a file can be appended to
  tryToWriteFile (filePath$) – check whether a file can be written (destructive!)
  writeFile (filePath$, ...) – create a new text file, and write texts, numbers, vectors and so on into it
  writeFileLine (filePath$, ...) – create a new text file, write texts, numbers, vectors and so on into it, followed by a newline
  writeInfo (...) – write texts, numbers, vectors and so on, to a clear Info window
  writeInfoLine (...) – write texts, numbers, vectors and so on, followed by a newline, to a clear Info window

# --- Conversion (acoustic/psychoacoustic) (10) ---
  barkToHertz (x) – from Bark-rate to acoustic frequency
  erbToHertz (x) – from ERB-rate to acoustic frequency
  hertzToBark (x) – from acoustic frequency to Bark-rate
  hertzToErb (x) – from acoustic frequency to ERB-rate
  hertzToMel (x) – from acoustic frequency to mel
  hertzToSemitones (x) – from acoustic frequency to logarithmic scale re 100 Hz
  melToHertz (x) – from mel to acoustic frequency
  phonToDifferenceLimens (phon) – from perceptual loudness to jnd-scale
  semitonesToHertz (x) – from logarithmic scale re 100 Hz to acoustic frequency
  soundPressureToPhon (frequency, soundPressure) – convert sound pressure level to phon (loudness level)

# --- Demo window (14) ---
  demoClicked ( ) – determine whether the user clicked in the Demo window
  demoClickedIn (xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax) – determine whether the user clicked in a rectangular region in the Demo window
  demoCommandKeyPressed ( ) – determine whether the user pressed the Command key when they typed into the Demo window
  demoInput (characters$) – determine whether the user typed (or clicked) the specified characters into the Demo window
  demoKey$ ( ) – determine the key that the user typed into the Demo window
  demoKeyPressed ( ) – determine whether the user typed anything into the Demo window
  demoOptionKeyPressed ( ) – determine whether the user pressed the Option key when they typed into the Demo window
  demoPeekInput ( ) – see whether a user event (click or key press) is available in the Demo window
  demoShiftKeyPressed ( ) – determine whether the user pressed the Shift key when they typed into the Demo window
  demoShow ( ) – make all deferred drawing commands immediately visible in the Demo window
  demoWaitForInput ( ) – wait for a user event (click or key press) in the Demo window
  demoWindowTitle (newTitle$) – change the title of the Demo window
  demoX ( ) – the horizontal position of a mouse click in the Demo window
  demoY ( ) – the vertical position of a mouse click in the Demo window

# --- Formula context attributes (18) ---
  col – the column number (of the current cell) in a Formula command  [attr]
  col$ [i] – the name of column i of an object  [attr]
  ncol – the number of columns in a matrix object or Matrix-like object  [attr]
  nrow – the number of rows in a matrix object or Matrix-like object  [attr]
  object (id) – the object with the given ID, as a matrix, vector, string  [attr]
  object# (id) – the object with the given ID, as a vector  [attr]
  object## (id) – the object with the given ID, as a matrix  [attr]
  object$ (id) – the name of the object with the given ID  [attr]
  object$# (id) – the object with the given ID, as a string array  [attr]
  row – the row number (of the current cell) in a Formula command  [attr]
  row# (matrix##, rowNumber) - extract one row from a matrix  [attr]
  row$ [i] – the name of row i of an object  [attr]
  x – the horizontal place (in world coordinates) of the current cell in a Formula command  [attr]
  xmax – the top of the horizontal domain of an object  [attr]
  xmin – the bottom of the horizontal domain of an object  [attr]
  y – the vertical place (in world coordinates) of the current cell in a Formula command  [attr]
  ymax – the top of the vertical domain of an object  [attr]
  ymin – the bottom of the vertical domain of an object  [attr]

# --- Scripting keywords (not Formula functions) (6) ---
  asynchronous – let the script continue while the sound is playing or a subprocess is running  [keyword]
  clearinfo – clear the Info window (no parentheses, no arguments)  [keyword]
  demo – execute a graphics command in the Demo window (keyword prefix, not a function; see COMMANDS_DemoWindow.txt)  [keyword]
  endeditor – leave an editor environment (usually found inside a script)  [keyword]
  endproc – end a procedure definition  [keyword]
  procedure – start a procedure definition  [keyword]

# --- Other (32) ---
  appDay ( ) – the month day at which the present version of Praat was built
  appMonth ( ) – the month in which the present version of Praat was built (between 1 and 12)

  appVersion ( ) – the number of the present version of Praat
  appVersion$ ( ) – the present version of Praat, as text
  appYear ( ) – the year in which the present version of Praat was built
  assert condition – condition checking
  asserterror message$ – testing that a certain error occurs
  besselI (n, x) – modified Bessel function of the first kind, In
  besselK (n, x) – modified Bessel function of the second kind, Kn
  chooseDirectory$ (title$) – file selector window for directories
  chooseReadFile$ (title$) – file selector window for reading
  chooseWriteFile$ (title$, defaultFilename$) – file selector window for writing
  createDirectory (path$) – create a new directory (also known as a folder)
  deleteFile (path$) – delete a file
  differenceLimensToPhon (dl) – from jnd-scale to perceptual loudness
  editor (...) – enter an editor environment (usually found inside a script)
  environment$ (environmentVariableName$) – look up a system environment variable
  exitScript (...) – show a message and terminate the script
  from_to# (from, to) – the integers from from through to
  from_to_by# (from, to, by) – numbers from from through to in steps of by
  from_to_count# (from, to, n) – n numbers from from through to
  gaussP (z) – area under the normal curve up to z
  gaussQ (z) – area under the normal curve after z
  invBinomialP (P, k, n) – inverse of binomialP
  invBinomialQ (Q, k, n) – inverse of binomialQ
  invGaussQ (q) – inverse of gaussQ
  newline$ – the newline symbol
  pauseScript (...) – show a message and pause the script
  rectify (x) – set to zero if negative (no change if positive)
  rectify# (vector#) – rectify each element of vector#
  rectify## (matrix##) – rectify each cell of matrix##
